<analysis>**original_problem_statement**:
The user initially requested the development of an enterprise-grade CVE (Common Vulnerabilities and Exposures) management platform. The project was divided into phases, with the most recent work focusing on implementing a CVE Ownership model.

However, during this session, the user pivoted and provided detailed specifications to create a complete, end-to-end infrastructure automation pipeline for CVE remediation. This new request involved setting up Terraform for multiple environments, creating a remediation Lambda function, and configuring a CI/CD workflow for building and deploying the Lambda.

PRODUCT REQUIREMENTS:
- **CVE Platform (Original Goal):**
    - Phase 1-4: Completed (Ownership model is pending user verification).

- **Infrastructure Automation (New Request):**
    - Create Terraform configurations for , , and  environments.

    - Create a packaging script for the Lambda function.
    - Create a GitHub Actions workflow to build and upload the Lambda artifact to S3.

**User's preferred language**: English

**what currently exists?**
The existing full-stack CVE Management Platform (React + FastAPI) is fully functional. In addition, a complete set of Infrastructure-as-Code (IaC) artifacts has been created to automate the deployment of a CVE remediation Lambda function. This includes Terraform configuration files, the Lambda source code with a packaging script, and a GitHub Actions workflow file.
